IT is hereby notified that His Excellency the President of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and
Commander - in - chief of the Armed Forces has been graciously pleased to approve the awarding of the Videsa Seva
Clasp in terms of regulation four of the proclamation instating, constituting and creating the Videsa Seva Clasp
Published in the Gazette Extraordinary, No.156/5 of 01st September 1981 to the person named in the schedule hereto.
        By His Excellency’s Command,
KAPILA WAIDY ARATHNE, P. C.,
Secretary,
Ministry of Defence.
At Colombo,
30th July, 2018.
SHEDULE
THE VIDESA SEV A CLASP

PART I : SEC. (I) - GAZETTE   EXTRAORDINARY   OF   THE   DEMOCRATIC   SOCIALIST   REPUBLIC   OF   SRI  LANKA 15.11.2018
102A
 THE UTTAMA SEV A PADAKKAMA
It is here by notified that His Excellency the President of the Democratic  Socialist Republic of  Sri Lanka and the
Commander in Chief of the Armed Forces has been graciously pleased to award the Uttama Seva Padakkama for the
year Two Thousand Sixteen in terms  of regulation four of the Presidential Warrant instituting, constituting and
creating the Uttam Seva Paddakkama published in the Government Gazette Extraordinary No: 156/5 of 01st September,
1981 to the persons named in the schedule hereto.
  By His Excellency’s Command,
KAPILA WAIDY ARATHNE, P. C.,
Secretary,
Ministry of Defence.
At Colombo,
11th November, 2018.
SHEDULE
